      "keystrokes": "cat > /app/steal.py << 'ENDOFFILE'\nimport numpy as np\nfrom forward import forward\n\n# Recover A1 by probing f(t*e_j) along basis directions\n# \n# Method:\n# 1. For each basis direction e_j, find breakpoints of g(t) = f(t*e_j)\n# 2. For each breakpoint, compute gradient of f just before and after\n# 3. The difference in gradients equals ±A2[i] * A1[i,:] for some neuron i\n# 4. Collect all these gradient-difference vectors and cluster them\n# 5. Each cluster corresponds to a row of A1 (up to scaling)\n\ndef num_grad(x):\n    \"\"\"Compute gradient of f at point x using central differences.\"\"\"\n    h = 1e-6\n    grad = np.zeros(10)\n    for j in range(10):\n        x_plus = x.copy()\n        x_plus[j] += h\n        x_minus = x.copy()\n        x_minus[j] -= h\n        grad[j] = (forward(x_plus) - forward(x_minus)) / (2 * h)\n    return grad\n\n\ndef find_breakpoints_1d(j, search_range=5.0, num_samples=10000):\n    \"\"\"Find breakpoints along basis direction j.\"\"\"\n    e_j = np.zeros(10)\n    e_j[j] = 1.0\n    t_vals = np.linspace(-search_range, search_range, num_samples)\n    dt = t_vals[1] - t_vals[0]\n    f_vals = np.array([forward(e_j * t) for t in t_vals])\n    forward_slopes = (f_vals[1:] - f_vals[:-1]) / dt\n    changes = np.diff(forward_slopes)\n    abs_changes = np.abs(changes)\n    \n    threshold = 1e-5\n    significant = np.where(abs_changes > threshold)[0]\n    \n    breakpoints = []\n    i = 0\n    while i < len(significant):\n        idx = significant[i]\n        if idx + 1 < len(changes) and abs_changes[idx+1] > threshold and np.sign(changes[idx]) == np.sign(changes[idx+1]):\n            c0 = changes[idx]\n            c1 = changes[idx+1]\n            total_change = c0 + c1\n            if abs(total_change) > 1e-10:\n                t_break = t_vals[idx+1] + dt * c0 / total_change\n                delta = total_change\n                breakpoints.append((t_break, delta))\n                i += 2\n                continue\n        i += 1\n    return breakpoints\n\n\ndef recover_A1():\n    \"\"\"Recover A1 matrix using only forward() queries.\"\"\"\n    \n    # diff is proportional to a row of A1\n            norm = np.linalg.norm(diff)\n            if norm > 1e-10:\n                row_vectors.append(diff / norm)\n                print(f\"    t={t_star:+.10f}, Δ={delta:+.8f}, row_vec_norm={norm:.6f}\")\n    \n    print(f\"\\nTotal row vectors collected: {len(row_vectors)}\")\n    \n    if len(row_vectors) < 20:\n        print(\"ERROR: Not enough vectors.\")\n        # Try with smaller threshold?\n        return None\n    \n    # Cluster the row vectors\n    # Each neuron should contribute multiple vectors (one per direction with non-zero A1)\n    # We need to find the unique directions\n    \n    # Average the vectors in this cluster\n        avg_vec = np.mean([vecs[i] for i in cluster], axis=0)\n        # Normalize\n        norm = np.linalg.norm(avg_vec)\n        if norm > 0:\n            A1_recovered[k, :] = avg_vec / norm\n        print(f\"  Cluster {k}: size={len(cluster)}\")\n    \n    return A1_recovered\n\n\nif __name__ == '__main__':\n    A1_stolen = recover_A1()\n    if A1_stolen is not None and A1_stolen.shape[0] > 0:\n        np.save('/app/stolen_A1.npy', A1_stolen)\n        print(f\"\\nSaved stolen A1 to /app/stolen_A1.npy\")\n        print(f\"Shape: {A1_stolen.shape}\")\n        print(\"Stolen A1 (rows normalized):\")\n        np.set_printoptions(precision=6, suppress=True, linewidth=200)\n        print(A1_stolen)\n        print(\"\\nDone!\")\n    else:\n        print(\"Failed to recover A1\")\nENDOFFILE\n",
